	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageRotatorTop-1');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageRotatorTop');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageRotatorTop' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageSectionsBetweenArticles-XFFIlJX-0D');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageSectionsBetweenArticles');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsBetweenArticles' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageSectionsBetweenArticles-6COW6Kn6Bg');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageSectionsBetweenArticles');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsBetweenArticles' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageSectionsSidebar450x250-6COW6Kn6Bg');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageSectionsSidebar450x250');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsSidebar450x250' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageSectionsSidebar500-PkDkhlce6u');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageSectionsSidebar500');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsSidebar500' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsBetweenArticles' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

      </div>
    </div>
  
</div>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageSectionsSidebar500-UuyUWjA7JM');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageSectionsSidebar500');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsSidebar500' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageSectionsBetweenArticles-OELsBRAzYS');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageSectionsBetweenArticles');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageSectionsBetweenArticles' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-homePageBetweenSections-eASmYZg4ne');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=homePageBetweenSections');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'homePageBetweenSections' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>

<script>
	async function renderAd() {
		let elementAd = document.getElementById('render-ad-welcomeScreening-1');
	  let response = await fetch('https://silesia24.pl/ad-manager/ads/render-ad?groupHandle=welcomeScreening');
	  if (response.status === 200) {
	    let data = await response.text();
	    if(data){
	    	if(elementAd.innerHTML === ""){
				  const scriptEl = document.createRange().createContextualFragment(data);
				  elementAd.appendChild(scriptEl);

					function adLazyLoad() {
						elementAd.querySelectorAll('img.lazyload').forEach(img => {
							img.setAttribute('src', img.getAttribute('data-srcset'));
							img.classList.remove('lazyload');
							img.classList.add('lazyloaded');
						});
					}

					window.addEventListener('mousemove', adLazyLoad);
					window.addEventListener('scroll', adLazyLoad);
	  		}
	    }
	  }
	}

	function start(callback) {
		// Exclude welcome screening from foto gallery
		let mainSection = null;
		let maxCount = 50;

		let checkMainSection = setInterval(function(){
			mainSection = document.querySelector('main');
			maxCount--;

			if(maxCount == 0) {
				clearInterval(checkMainSection);
				return;
			}

			if(mainSection == null || mainSection == undefined) return;

			clearInterval(checkMainSection);

			if(mainSection.classList.contains('fotoGalleryPage') && 'welcomeScreening' == 'welcomeScreening') return;
			callback();
		}, 100);
	}

	start(renderAd);
</script>
